window.onerror = function onErrorFunc(msg, url, line, colno, error) {
if(!window.ta || !ta.has('ta.js_error_array.processed')) {
if(typeof js_error_array == 'undefined') {
js_error_array = [];
}
var err = error;
js_error_array[js_error_array.length] = {'msg': msg, 'error_script': url, 'line': line, 'column': colno, 'error': err, 'ready_state': document.readyState};
return true;
}
else {
if(window.ta && ta.util && ta.util.error && ta.util.error.record) {
ta.util.error.record(error, 'error post load:: ' + msg, null, {'error_script': url, 'line': line, 'column': colno, 'ready_state': document.readyState});
}
}
};
</script>

ta.store('moduleAjax', moduleAjax);
moduleAjax.register('modules.travelmap.LWTravelmap');
moduleAjax.register('modules.common.BackToTop');
moduleAjax.register('modules.membercenter.DestinationExpert');
moduleAjax.register('modules.travelmap.PinFlyout');
moduleAjax.register('modules.membercenter.MemberProfileLinks');
moduleAjax.register('modules.membercenter.PublicHeader');
moduleAjax.register('modules.membercenter.CityTiles');
moduleAjax.register('modules.common.PinCounts');
moduleAjax.register('modules.common.ExploreLinks');
moduleAjax.register('modules.membercenter.ReviewBadges');
moduleAjax.register('modules.membercenter.AboutMe');
moduleAjax.register('modules.membercenter.TravelStats');
ox.AbstractData.prototype.moduleAjax = moduleAjax;
ta.keep('facebook.onSessionAvail', function(){
var member = oxapp.context.has('LoggedInMember') && oxapp.context.get('LoggedInMember');
var fbId = member && member.get('data') && member.get('data.facebook_id') || null;
if (fbId != ta.retrieve('fb.auth.userId')) {
moduleAjax.fire ( "LOGIN", {} );
}
});
}());
